### "The Ghost of Ellis County"
This is an apt description. Rebecca Herzog has the smallest public footprint of any elected official in Ellis County. After exhaustive searching:

- **No biography found** in any news article, candidate profile, or public record
- **No campaign website found**
- **No social media presence found** (no Facebook, LinkedIn, Twitter, Instagram)
- **No news interviews found**
- **No candidate Q&A found** (unlike commissioner and clerk candidates who participated in Hays Post profiles)
- **No photos found** outside of the Ellis County website
- **No education, family, or personal information found** in any public source
- **No campaign materials found** -- she apparently won with zero public-facing campaign
- The only publicly accessible information is her office contact information and election results

### What We Know
1. She has worked in the Ellis County Register of Deeds office since approximately 2016
2. She was elected in 2024 as a Republican
3. She received 7,074 votes
4. She processes property records, deeds, and land ownership documents for Ellis County
5. She has a phone number and an email address

### Assessment
Rebecca Herzog is genuinely invisible in the public sphere. In an era of social media, candidate profiles, and local news coverage of every election, she managed to win an elected office without leaving a single searchable trace of her personal life, campaign, or views. This is either extraordinary privacy discipline or a reflection of how uncontested Register of Deeds races work in rural Kansas -- the office is so non-political that no one asks questions, and no one campaigns. She is, indeed, the Ghost of Ellis County.

### Sources
- [Ellis County: Register of Deeds](https://www.ellisco.net/100/Register-of-Deeds)
- [Kansas Register of Deeds Association](https://ksrods.com/contact-information/ellis-county-el-nc-district/)
- [Hays Post: 2024 election results](https://hayspost.com/posts/1873ff67-3bab-44c2-896b-8aee3a992496)

# APPENDIX: NRSC ETHICS INVESTIGATION (March 2026)

The National Republican Senatorial Committee called on the Senate Select Committee on Ethics to investigate four Kansas Democratic Senate candidates for allegedly failing to submit required financial disclosures within the federal timeframe:

1. **Erik Murray** -- Campaign attributed delays to federal government shutdown complications affecting FEC systems
2. **Sandy Spidel Neumann** -- Status of response not confirmed
3. **Christy Davis** -- Status of response not confirmed
4. **Anne Parelkar** -- Status of response not confirmed

This is likely a political tactic by the NRSC (standard opposition practice) rather than a substantive legal threat, but it creates negative headlines for the affected candidates.

**Source:** [KSN: Candidates under scrutiny](https://www.ksn.com/news/state-regional/kansas-us-senate-candidates-under-scrutiny-over-missing-financial-disclosures/)

## CODEX DEEP RESEARCH 2026-04-01

### Verified Identity
- Roger Wayne Marshall, M.D.
- Republican U.S. senator for Kansas, first elected in 2020 and in office since January 2021.
- Born in El Dorado, Kansas, raised in a farm family, and long associated with Great Bend.

### Bio
Marshall built his public career around medicine, rural identity, and conservative social politics. He trained as a physician, practiced OB/GYN in Great Bend for more than 25 years, and repeatedly frames himself as a Kansas doctor who brought local, practical experience into Washington. He remains deeply tied to the Great Bend area and to the larger western-Kansas rural worldview that animates much of his messaging.

His official and campaign materials emphasize that he is not a transactional Washington figure but a small-town Kansan who stayed rooted in local institutions. That record matters in this file because it is unusually well documented: church leadership, medical practice, military reserve service, and civic board work all reinforce the same identity narrative.

### Record / Actions
- Served in the U.S. Army Reserve, then completed medical training and built a long OB/GYN practice in Great Bend.
- Delivered more than 5,000 babies, a fact he routinely ties to his pro-life stance.
- Won the Kansas Senate seat in 2020 after serving in the U.S. House from 2017 to 2021.
- In 2025-2026 he remained closely associated with Trump-aligned messaging on budget cuts, border policy, Ukraine aid, and DOGE.
- The Oakley town hall walkout became a durable vulnerability after he left early and then characterized attendees as "paid Democratic operatives."

### Verbatim Quotes
- "Delivering for Kansas." - campaign site, n.d., https://kansansformarshall.com/ (campaign slogan)
- "abortion is wrong at any stage" - campaign life page, n.d., https://kansansformarshall.com/life (abortion)
- "Look, I was wrong." - The Hill, March 2026, https://thehill.com/homenews/senate/5778492-roger-marshall-iran-nuclear-program-comments/ (Iran walkback)
- "We cannot continue selling our grandchildren down a river..." - Senate press release, April 2024, https://www.marshall.senate.gov/newsroom/press-releases/senator-marshall-releases-statement-on-foreign-aid-bill/ (Ukraine aid)

### Faith / Church
- Verified congregation: First Christian Church, Great Bend, Kansas.
- Denominational identity: Christian Church (Disciples of Christ), often described publicly as nondenominational Christian in his own bios.
- Public leadership record: elder, deacon, board chairman, and Sunday school teacher with wife Laina for more than 25 years.
- Church URLs found: https://www.firstchristianchurchgb.com/ and https://kansasdisciples.org/property/great-bend-first-christian-church/

### Campaign Finance
- FEC candidate page: https://www.fec.gov/data/candidate/S0KS00315/
- FEC committee page: https://www.fec.gov/data/committee/C00576173/?cycle=2026
- Public FEC summary shows total receipts of $4,759,694.80 and ending cash on hand of $4,072,295.56 through 2025-12-31.
- 2025 receipts alone were $2,563,147.27, with $195,870.35 in disbursements.
- Public donor notes from prior research: Koch Industries PAC $10,000, Spirit AeroSystems PAC $10,000, and U.S. Chamber of Commerce IE support of roughly $1.9M.

### Controversies / Notable Facts
- Left the Oakley town hall early and his team claimed the crowd was made up of "paid Democratic operatives."
- Was publicly pressed after Iran comments and admitted, "Look, I was wrong."
- He remains one of the most reliable Trump-aligned votes in the Kansas delegation, which keeps him politically secure but also highly polarizing.
- His faith record is unusually deep and sustained compared with most candidates in the project.

## PASS 1: BIOGRAPHY & PERSONAL BACKGROUND

### Birth & Early Life
- **Full Name**: Roger Wayne Marshall

- First in his family to attend college

### Education
- **A.S.**: Butler Community College, 1980
- **B.S.**: Biochemistry, Kansas State University
- **M.D.**: University of Kansas School of Medicine, 1987
- **Residency**: Obstetrics & Gynecology, Bayfront Medical Center, St. Petersburg, Florida

### Military Service
- U.S. Army Reserve, 1984-1991 (7 years)

### Family
- **Wife**: Laina Marshall — married 40+ years
- **Children**: 4 children
- **Grandchildren**: 4 grandchildren

### Church & Faith
- **Denomination**: Nondenominational Christian

- **Leadership Roles**: Elder, deacon, board chairman
- Taught Sunday school with wife Laina for over 25 years
- Accepted Christ at a Fellowship of Christian Athletes event in high school
- Committed to daily Bible reading
- 2016 campaign stated goal: bring "small-town Christian values" to Washington, D.C.

### Community Involvement
- Chairman of the Board, Great Bend Regional Hospital
- Vice President, Farmers Bank and Trust
- District Governor, Rotary International

## PASS 3: VOTING RECORD & SCORECARD RATINGS

### Committee Assignments
- Senate Agriculture, Nutrition, & Forestry
- Senate Finance
- Senate Budget
- Senate Health, Education, Labor, & Pensions (HELP)

### Scorecard Ratings
- **Heritage Action**: 94% (117th Congress), 89% (118th Congress)
- **NRA**: A+ rating — Lifetime NRA member
- **National Pro-Life Scorecard (SBA Pro-Life America)**: Consistent pro-life voting record
- **League of Conservation Voters**: Low score (specific number requires direct page access)
- **AFL-CIO**: Low score (consistently votes against labor priorities)

### Key Votes — Abortion / Life Issues
- Opposes abortion including in cases of rape and incest
- Called for overturning Roe v. Wade (2020)
- Voted against Women's Health Protection Act (May 2022) — called it "immoral" and "horrific"
- Supported Value Them Both Amendment in Kansas (defeated August 2022)
- Lifetime member, American Association of Pro-Life OB/GYNs
- Gave Senate floor speeches defending life on eve of Dobbs decision

### Key Votes — Gun Policy
- NRA A+ rating
- Voted AGAINST bipartisan gun reform legislation (June 2022)
- Opposes red flag laws, "assault weapon" bans, and buyback programs
- Introduced "Home Defense and Competitive Shooting Act" (removes short-barreled rifles from NFA)
- Supported Fix NICS Act (strengthening background check reporting — signed into law)
- Introduced Safe Schools Act (18 Senate cosponsors)

### Key Votes — Immigration
- Opposes path to citizenship for DACA participants
- Cosponsored Secure the Border Act of 2023
- Voted against bipartisan border bill (2024) — sided with Trump-aligned opposition
- Led no-confidence vote effort against DHS Secretary Mayorkas
- Called for immediate passage of H.R. 2 (Secure Our Borders Act)
- Wants "wall" built, opposes "magnets" attracting migrants

### Key Votes — Foreign Aid / Defense
- Voted AGAINST $95.3 billion aid package for Ukraine, Israel, and Taiwan (April 2024)
  - Was one of only 18 senators to vote no
  - Opposed Ukraine funding specifically: "We cannot continue selling our grandchildren down a river and sending another $60 billion we do not have to Ukraine"
  - Supported Israel aid alone, tried to separate Israel funding
  - Fellow Kansas Senator Jerry Moran voted YES — they diverged on this vote
- Opposed additional Ukraine aid in early 2025

### Key Votes — Healthcare
- Opposed Biden vaccine mandates for healthcare workers
- Opposed mask mandates
- Introduced FAUCI Act (after Fauci hot mic incident)
- Pushed for CDC reform and "restoring trust"
- Advocated for disease prevention focus
- Supported medical price transparency initiatives

### Key Votes — Agriculture
- Introduced ACE Agriculture Act of 2026 (S. 3637)
- Serves on Agriculture Committee — central to legislative portfolio
- Praised Trump administration's Renewable Fuel Standard rule (March 2026)

### Key Votes — Budget / Spending
- Introduced comprehensive budget process reform legislation (June 2025)
- Quote: "With the U.S. national debt exceeding $36 trillion, it's clear that the federal budgeting process is a dysfunctional mess"

## PASS 7: JANUARY 6 / ELECTION OBJECTIONS

### Pre-January 6 Position
- As Senator-Elect, announced in advance his intention to object to Electoral College certification
- Joined effort led by Senators Josh Hawley (MO) and Ted Cruz (TX)

### January 6, 2021 — The Votes
- **Arizona electors**: Voted YES on objection (one of 6 senators)
- **Pennsylvania electors**: Voted YES on objection (one of 7 senators)
- Was one of only 8 Republican senators total who voted to object to any state's electors

### Post-January 6 Statements
- Same night (January 7, 2021): Acknowledged Joe Biden as the victor of the General Election
- May 2021 (CNN interview): "I was concerned then and I still am today that six states broke their own laws or their own constitution, but it's time to move on."
- CNN headline: "A Republican senator who voted for the Big Lie now thinks we should all just move on"

### Accountability Tracking

## PASS 8: HEALTHCARE POSITIONS & COVID RESPONSE

### COVID-19 Stance
- Stated he is "not anti-vaccine" and believes MMR, DPT, and polio vaccines are "great vaccines"
- Said "I do think the vaccines work. I'm not convinced the masks really work at all."
- Believes "some people need a Covid vaccine and some don't"
- Recommended hydroxychloroquine during early pandemic despite limited evidence
- Appeared with other doctors urging vaccine consideration, but inconsistent messaging
- KCUR headline: "Kansas Senator Roger Marshall Is A Doctor, But His COVID-19 Advice Doesn't Always Sound Like It"
- Critics called his COVID statements "dangerous"

### Vaccine Mandates
- Led opposition to Biden's vaccine mandate for healthcare workers (with Sen. Blackburn and others)
- Position: Vaccine choice is between individuals and their doctors, not government mandates
- Pushed for "vaccine transparency" rather than mandates
- Not every child needs a COVID vaccine, per his statements

### Fauci Confrontation (January 2022)
- During Senate HELP Committee hearing, demanded Fauci's financial disclosures
- Fauci said his disclosures were already public
- Hot mic caught Fauci calling Marshall "a moron" and muttering "Jesus Christ"
- Marshall responded: "Calling me a moron during a Senate hearing may have alleviated the stress of the least trusted bureaucrat in America, but it didn't take away from the facts."
- Introduced FAUCI Act (Financial Accountability for Uniquely Compensated Individuals) requiring top government officials to publicly disclose financial records
- Published Fauci's "previously unpublished financial records" from his office

### Other Healthcare Positions
- Advocates disease prevention over treatment
- Pushes medical price transparency
- Introduced 21st Century WIC Act of 2026 (S. 3842)
- Introduced Healthy Start Reauthorization Act of 2026 (S. 3799)
- Called for "bringing common sense back to medicine"
- Called for "restoring trust in the CDC"

- [KCUR - COVID Advice](https://www.kcur.org/news/2021-08-26/kansas-senator-roger-marshall-is-a-doctor-but-his-covid-19-advice-doesnt-always-sound-like-it) — accessed 2026-03-30
- [Newsweek - Fauci Moron Response](https://www.newsweek.com/roger-marshall-responds-fauci-calling-him-moron-1668391) — accessed 2026-03-30
- [CBS News - Fauci Hot Mic](https://www.cbsnews.com/news/anthony-fauci-roger-marshall-hot-mic-moron/) — accessed 2026-03-30
- [The Hill - Fauci Spars](https://thehill.com/homenews/senate/589249-hot-mic-catches-fauci-calling-gop-senator-a-moron/) — accessed 2026-03-30
- [marshall.senate.gov - Fauci Response](https://www.marshall.senate.gov/newsroom/press-releases/sen-marshall-responds-to-dr-fauci-hot-mic-situation/) — accessed 2026-03-30

## PASS 9: 2026 CHALLENGERS

### Republican Primary
- **Roger Marshall** (incumbent) — endorsed by Trump, Senate Conservatives Fund
- **Chase LaPorte** — Republican primary challenger (limited public profile)

### Democratic Primary (8 candidates as of March 2026)
Primary: August 4, 2026

1. **Jason Hart** — Former federal prosecutor (Assistant U.S. Attorney, District of Kansas). Specialized in child exploitation and cybercrime. Quit his position and switched party affiliation to join the race (early March 2026). Recent entry to the race.
   - Source: [KMUW - Opens Arms to Republicans](https://www.kmuw.org/government/2026-03-25/democratic-candidate-in-u-s-senate-race-opens-arms-to-kansas-republicans-lost-in-the-wilderness)

2. **Anne Parelkar** — Immigration attorney, Overland Park. Never held public office.
   - Source: [Kansas Reflector - Democratic Candidate](https://kansasreflector.com/2025/08/18/democratic-u-s-senate-candidate-eager-to-broaden-kansas-voice-in-d-c-politics/)

3. **Christy Davis** — Cottonwood Falls. Kansas director for USDA Rural Development under President Biden. Previously ran for KS-01 in 2020 (unsuccessful).
   - Source: [KCUR Candidate Guide](https://www.kcur.org/politics-elections-and-government/2025-12-30/whos-running-to-represent-kansas-in-the-u-s-senate-in-2026-heres-a-guide-to-the-candidates)

4. **Sandy Spidel Neumann** — Mission, KS. Former financial services executive. No prior public office.
   - Source: [Kansas Reflector - Democrats Sharpen Attack](https://kansasreflector.com/2025/11/25/kansas-democratic-candidates-for-u-s-senate-sharpen-attack-on-gop-incumbent-roger-marshall/)

5. **Erik Murray** — Commercial real estate developer.
   - Source: [Kansas Reflector - Kansas City Entrepreneur](https://kansasreflector.com/2026/03/16/kansas-city-entrepreneur-prioritizes-passion-decency-in-campaign-for-u-s-senate/)

6. **Michael Soetaert** — Art gallery owner. Former city council member, Wellington, KS.
   - Source: [KCUR Candidate Guide](https://www.kcur.org/politics-elections-and-government/2025-12-30/whos-running-to-represent-kansas-in-the-u-s-senate-in-2026-heres-a-guide-to-the-candidates)

7. **Patrick Schmidt** — Kansas state senator.
   - Source: [Wikipedia - 2026 KS Senate Election](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2026_United_States_Senate_election_in_Kansas)

8. **Noah Tyler** — Counterintelligence specialist.
   - Source: [Wikipedia - 2026 KS Senate Election](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2026_United_States_Senate_election_in_Kansas)

### Race Context
- Kansas has not elected a Democrat to the U.S. Senate since 1932 (nearly a century)
- Marshall won 2020 general election with 53.2%
- Democratic candidates are positioning around cost-of-living, DOGE cuts, agricultural funding, and healthcare
- Primary election: August 4, 2026

## PASS 11: BILLS SPONSORED & LEGISLATION

### Signature Legislation
1. **Credit Card Competition Act** (S. 3623, 2026; previously introduced in prior Congresses)
   - Bipartisan bill with Sen. Dick Durbin (D-IL) and Sen. Peter Welch (D-VT)
   - Requires large banks ($100B+ assets) to enable at least 2 unaffiliated card networks
   - Breaks Visa-Mastercard duopoly on swipe fees
   - Endorsed by Trump on Truth Social (January 2026)
   - Pushed as amendment to crypto bill, then dropped

2. **FAUCI Act** (Financial Accountability for Uniquely Compensated Individuals)
   - Introduced after Fauci hot mic incident
   - Requires top government officials to publicly disclose financial records

3. **ACE Agriculture Act of 2026** (S. 3637)
   - Agriculture-focused legislation from Agriculture Committee

4. **21st Century WIC Act of 2026** (S. 3842)
   - Modernizes WIC nutrition program

5. **Healthy Start Reauthorization Act of 2026** (S. 3799)
   - Healthcare maternal/infant health program reauthorization

6. **WALZ Act** (S. 3642)
   - Details not fully available from search results

7. **Public Charge Clarification Act of 2026** (S. 3602)
   - Immigration-related — clarifies public charge rules

8. **Home Defense and Competitive Shooting Act**
   - Removes short-barreled rifles from NFA purview

9. **Safe Schools Act**
   - School safety legislation — 18 Senate cosponsors

10. **Comprehensive Budget Process Reform** (introduced June 2025)
    - Overhaul of federal budgeting process

### Legislative Statistics (GovTrack 2024)
- Got the 2nd most cosponsors on bills compared to Senate Sophomores

**Sources**:
- [GovTrack - Roger Marshall](https://www.govtrack.us/congress/members/roger_marshall/412704) — accessed 2026-03-30
- [Durbin/Marshall - Credit Card Competition Act](https://www.durbin.senate.gov/newsroom/press-releases/durbin-marshall-reintroduce-the-credit-card-competition-act) — accessed 2026-03-30
- [marshall.senate.gov - Credit Card Competition Act](https://www.marshall.senate.gov/newsroom/press-releases/marshall-durbin-reintroduce-credit-card-competition-act-backed-by-president-trump/) — accessed 2026-03-30
- [marshall.senate.gov - Budget Reform](https://www.marshall.senate.gov/newsroom/press-releases/senator-marshall-introduces-comprehensive-bill-to-reform-americas-dysfunctional-budget-process/) — accessed 2026-03-30

## PASS 12: VERBATIM QUOTES

### On Trump's Joint Address (March 6, 2025)
> "The theme of last night's speech was 'Renewal of the American Dream,' and it could have also been called 'Promises Made, Promises Kept.' Since he took office, President Trump has been working hard to deliver on the promises he made during the 2024 election. His Administration is securing our border, deporting criminal aliens, eliminating waste, fraud, and abuse through the DOGE initiative, strengthening our economic position across the world through reciprocal tariffs and trade agreements, and pushing for an end to the destructive war in Ukraine."
— [marshall.senate.gov press release, March 6, 2025](https://www.marshall.senate.gov/newsroom/press-releases/senator-marshall-releases-statement-after-president-trumps-joint-address-to-congress/)

### On Budget Reform (June 17, 2025)
> "With the U.S. national debt exceeding $36 trillion, it's clear that the federal budgeting process is a dysfunctional mess. Congress continues to lurch from crisis to crisis without any long-term vision or accountability. Rather than continue to repeat the same missteps that have burdened us and our grandchildren with debt they can never repay, we need radical change."
— [marshall.senate.gov press release, June 17, 2025](https://www.marshall.senate.gov/newsroom/press-releases/senator-marshall-introduces-comprehensive-bill-to-reform-americas-dysfunctional-budget-process/)

### On Renewable Fuel Standard (March 28, 2026)
> "This is exactly what putting Kansas farmers first looks like. Thanks to President Trump and Administrator Lee Zeldin, our farmers now have more market access, more certainty, and a stronger future than ever before."
— [marshall.senate.gov press release, March 28, 2026](https://www.marshall.senate.gov/newsroom/press-releases/senator-marshall-praises-trump-admins-historic-renewable-fuel-standard-rule/)

### On Iran — The Walkback (March 2026)
> "Look, I was wrong."
— To CNN's Kaitlan Collins, admitting his previous claims about Trump's Operation "Midnight Hammer" destroying Iran's nuclear program were incorrect
— [The Hill, March 2026](https://thehill.com/homenews/senate/5778492-roger-marshall-iran-nuclear-program-comments/)
— [Mediaite](https://www.mediaite.com/media/news/republican-senator-says-i-was-wrong-when-confronted-with-past-claim-about-iran/)
— [Breitbart, March 11, 2026](https://www.breitbart.com/clips/2026/03/11/gop-sen-marshall-i-was-wrong-irans-program-wasnt-set-back-years-by-midnight-hammer/)

### On Fauci (January 2022)
> "Calling me a moron during a Senate hearing may have alleviated the stress of the least trusted bureaucrat in America, but it didn't take away from the facts. We need the truth Dr. Fauci!"
— [Response on Twitter after hot mic incident](https://www.marshall.senate.gov/newsroom/press-releases/sen-marshall-responds-to-dr-fauci-hot-mic-situation/)

### On January 6 / Election Objections (May 2021)
> "I was concerned then and I still am today that six states broke their own laws or their own constitution, but it's time to move on."
— [CNN, May 2021](https://amp.cnn.com/cnn/2021/05/03/politics/roger-marshall-january-6-cnn-big-lie/)

### On Ukraine Aid (April 2024)
> "We cannot continue selling our grandchildren down a river and sending another $60 billion we do not have to Ukraine."
— [marshall.senate.gov, April 2024](https://www.marshall.senate.gov/newsroom/press-releases/senator-marshall-releases-statement-on-foreign-aid-bill/)

### On Town Hall Attendees (March 2025)
- Called attendees "rude" before leaving 20 minutes early
- His chief of staff: "Democrat operatives that couldn't place Oakley, Kansas on a map before today sabotaged a local town hall."
— [KWCH, March 2025](https://www.kwch.com/2025/03/04/sen-marshall-doubles-down-decision-leave-town-hall-early-claim-that-it-was-sabotaged/)

### On Abortion (Campaign Website)
> States his position on life "has remained consistent — that abortion is wrong at any stage" as "a lifetime member of the American Association of Pro-Life OB/GYNs"
— [kansansformarshall.com/life](https://kansansformarshall.com/life)

## PASS 13: CONTROVERSIES

### 1. January 6 Election Objection (2021)
- **Severity**: HIGH
- One of 8 senators to vote against certifying 2020 election results
- Objected to both Arizona and Pennsylvania electors
- Later acknowledged Biden as president same night
- Later said "time to move on"
- Tracked by multiple accountability organizations

### 2. STOCK Act Violation (2021)
- **Severity**: MEDIUM
- Failed to timely disclose stock transactions made by his dependent children
- Transactions included up to $15,000 in Chevron and Disney stock during the 2020 pandemic market crash
- Disclosed 12-17 months late — well past the 45-day STOCK Act deadline
- Transactions happened Feb-July 2020 while he was in the House
- Part of broader pattern — Campaign Legal Center filed complaints against 13 members for STOCK Act violations that year

### 3. Reckless Driving Conviction Erasure (2008)
- **Severity**: MEDIUM-HIGH
- May 2008: Charged with reckless driving AND battery after allegedly hitting a Great Bend resident with his truck
- Convicted of reckless driving
- Sentenced to 5 days jail (suspended), $150 fine, $75 court costs
- December 24, 2008 (Christmas Eve): Assistant County Attorney Carey Fleske asked judge to erase the conviction and replace with lesser charge
- **Conflict of Interest**: Fleske was the son of Leonard T. Fleske, an orthopedic surgeon who co-founded a surgical center with Marshall in 2000. Both had 9.4% ownership stakes.
- Called "bizarre" and "very unusual" by legal observers
- Reported by Kansas City Star during 2020 Senate campaign

### 4. Oakley Town Hall Walkout (March 2025)
- **Severity**: MEDIUM
- Left town hall 20 minutes early after calling audience "rude"
- Claimed attendees were "paid Democratic operatives" and "paid troublemakers"
- Shared Trump's Truth Social post claiming "paid troublemakers" infiltrate Republican events
- Attendees identified as western Kansas farmers and concerned constituents — many in a county that voted overwhelmingly for Trump
- Farmers said they were there about unpaid federal contracts and USDA cuts
- Kansas Reflector challenged him to prove the "paid agitators" claim
- KCUR investigation found attendees were local concerned citizens

### 5. "I Was Wrong" Iran Walkback (March 2026)
- **Severity**: MEDIUM
- In June 2025, claimed on Fox News that Trump's Operation "Midnight Hammer" had destroyed Iran's nuclear program for years
- Confronted on CNN by Kaitlan Collins with his own clips
- Admitted "Look, I was wrong"
- Demonstrates pattern of making claims based on partisan talking points without verification

### 6. COVID Misinformation Concerns (2021)
- **Severity**: MEDIUM
- As a physician, recommended hydroxychloroquine despite limited evidence
- Gave inconsistent messages about vaccines and masks
- KCUR and KOAM reported his statements could be "dangerous"
- Opposed mask mandates while COVID was surging

### 7. Fauci Hot Mic Incident (January 2022)
- **Severity**: LOW (Marshall came out looking like the victim/winner politically)
- Fauci called him "a moron" on hot mic
- Marshall leveraged it into the FAUCI Act and published Fauci's financial records
- Politically beneficial for Marshall with his base

**Sources**:
- All sources cited in relevant passes above

## PASS 15: FINANCIAL DISCLOSURES & PROPERTY

### Net Worth
- **Estimated**: $6.0 million (as of September 2025, per Quiver Quantitative)
- **Range**: $2.26 million to $9.1 million (per 2023 financial disclosure filing ranges)
- **Congressional Rank**: 153rd highest net worth in Congress

### Major Holdings (Per Senate Financial Disclosures)
- **Farmers Enterprises, Inc., 1% Interest**: Up to $5,000,000 (non-public stock, held by spouse)
- **Ionics Life Sciences** (subscription agreement): Up to $500,000
- **AWSHX - Washington Mutual Investments Fund Cl A**: Up to $500,000
- **IDX Precision Strategies Using S&P 500 Index**: Up to $500,000
- **IDX Performance 3-Year Strategy S&P 500 Index**: Up to $250,000
- Substantial savings accounts, mutual funds, and real estate in rural Kansas

### Business Interests
- **Great Bend Surgical Center**: Co-founded in 2000 with Leonard T. Fleske and other physicians (9.4% ownership stake at time of 2008 driving incident)
- **Farmers Bank and Trust**: Served as Vice President
- **Farmers Enterprises, Inc.**: Spouse holds up to $5M interest — the most valuable disclosed asset

### STOCK Act Issues
- Dependent children purchased up to $15,000 in Chevron and Disney stock during 2020 pandemic crash
- Disclosed 12-17 months late, violating the 45-day STOCK Act reporting requirement
- Irony: Marshall later co-sponsored legislation to ban insider trading in Congress
